              <svg class="octicon octicon-device-desktop" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1.75 2.5h12.5a.25.25 0 01.25.25v7.5a.25.25 0 01-.25.25H1.75a.25.25 0 01-.25-.25v-7.5a.25.25 0 01.25-.25zM14.25 1H1.75A1.75 1.75 0 000 2.75v7.5C0 11.216.784 12 1.75 12h3.727c-.1 1.041-.52 1.872-1.292 2.757A.75.75 0 004.75 16h6.5a.75.75 0 00.565-1.243c-.772-.885-1.193-1.716-1.292-2.757h3.727A1.75 1.75 0 0016 10.25v-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0014.25 1zM9.018 12H6.982a5.72 5.72 0 01-.765 2.5h3.566a5.72 5.72 0 01-.765-2.5z"></path></svg>
          </a>

          <a href="/login?return_to=%2Fvuejs%2Fcn.vuejs.org%2Fblob%2Fmaster%2Fsrc%2Fv2%2Fapi%2Findex.md" class="btn-octicon disabled tooltipped tooltipped-nw"
            aria-label="You must be signed in to make or propose changes">
            <svg class="octicon octicon-pencil" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M11.013 1.427a1.75 1.75 0 012.474 0l1.086 1.086a1.75 1.75 0 010 2.474l-8.61 8.61c-.21.21-.47.364-.756.445l-3.251.93a.75.75 0 01-.927-.928l.929-3.25a1.75 1.75 0 01.445-.758l8.61-8.61zm1.414 1.06a.25.25 0 00-.354 0L10.811 3.75l1.439 1.44 1.263-1.263a.25.25 0 000-.354l-1.086-1.086zM11.189 6.25L9.75 4.81l-6.286 6.287a.25.25 0 00-.064.108l-.558 1.953 1.953-.558a.249.249 0 00.108-.064l6.286-6.286z"></path></svg>
          </a>
          <a href="/login?return_to=%2Fvuejs%2Fcn.vuejs.org%2Fblob%2Fmaster%2Fsrc%2Fv2%2Fapi%2Findex.md" class="btn-octicon btn-octicon-danger disabled tooltipped tooltipped-nw"
            aria-label="You must be signed in to make or propose changes">
            <svg class="octicon octicon-trashcan" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 1.75a.25.25 0 01.25-.25h2.5a.25.25 0 01.25.25V3h-3V1.75zm4.5 0V3h2.25a.75.75 0 010 1.5H2.75a.75.75 0 010-1.5H5V1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h2.5C10.216 0 11 .784 11 1.75zM4.496 6.675a.75.75 0 10-1.492.15l.66 6.6A1.75 1.75 0 005.405 15h5.19c.9 0 1.652-.681 1.741-1.576l.66-6.6a.75.75 0 00-1.492-.149l-.66 6.6a.25.25 0 01-.249.225h-5.19a.25.25 0 01-.249-.225l-.66-6.6z"></path></svg>
          </a>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

      
  <div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0">
    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><table data-table-type="yaml-metadata">
  <thead>
  <tr>
  <th>title</th>
  <th>type</th>
  </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
  <tr>
  <td><div>API</div></td>
  <td><div>api</div></td>
  </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

<h2><a id="user-content-全局配置" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#全局配置"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>全局配置</h2>
<p><code>Vue.config</code> 是一个对象，包含 Vue 的全局配置。可以在启动应用之前修改下列 property：</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-silent" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#silent"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>silent</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>boolean</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>默认值</strong>：<code>false</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">silent</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span></pre></div>
<p>取消 Vue 所有的日志与警告。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-optionmergestrategies" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#optionmergestrategies"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>optionMergeStrategies</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>{ [key: string]: Function }</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>默认值</strong>：<code>{}</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">optionMergeStrategies</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">_my_option</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">parent</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">child</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">child</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">Profile</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">extend</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">_my_option</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Profile.options._my_option = 2</span></pre></div>
<p>自定义合并策略的选项。</p>
<p>合并策略选项分别接收在父实例和子实例上定义的该选项的值作为第一个和第二个参数，Vue 实例上下文被作为第三个参数传入。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/mixins.html#%E8%87%AA%E5%AE%9A%E4%B9%89%E9%80%89%E9%A1%B9%E6%B7%B7%E5%85%A5%E7%AD%96%E7%95%A5">自定义选项的混入策略</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-devtools" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#devtools"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>devtools</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>boolean</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>默认值</strong>：<code>true</code> (生产版为 <code>false</code>)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-c">// 务必在加载 Vue 之后，立即同步设置以下内容</span>
<span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">devtools</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span></pre></div>
<p>配置是否允许 <a href="https://github.com/vuejs/vue-devtools">vue-devtools</a> 检查代码。开发版本默认为 <code>true</code>，生产版本默认为 <code>false</code>。生产版本设为 <code>true</code> 可以启用检查。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-errorhandler" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#errorhandler"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>errorHandler</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Function</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>默认值</strong>：<code>undefined</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">errorHandler</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">err</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">info</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// handle error</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// `info` 是 Vue 特定的错误信息，比如错误所在的生命周期钩子</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// 只在 2.2.0+ 可用</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p>指定组件的渲染和观察期间未捕获错误的处理函数。这个处理函数被调用时，可获取错误信息和 Vue 实例。</p>
<blockquote>
<p>从 2.2.0 起，这个钩子也会捕获组件生命周期钩子里的错误。同样的，当这个钩子是 <code>undefined</code> 时，被捕获的错误会通过 <code>console.error</code> 输出而避免应用崩溃。</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>从 2.4.0 起，这个钩子也会捕获 Vue 自定义事件处理函数内部的错误了。</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>从 2.6.0 起，这个钩子也会捕获 <code>v-on</code> DOM 监听器内部抛出的错误。另外，如果任何被覆盖的钩子或处理函数返回一个 Promise 链 (例如 async 函数)，则来自其 Promise 链的错误也会被处理。</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>错误追踪服务 <a href="https://sentry.io" rel="nofollow">Sentry</a> 和 <a href="https://docs.bugsnag.com/platforms/browsers/vue/" rel="nofollow">Bugsnag</a> 都通过此选项提供了官方支持。</p>
</blockquote>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-warnhandler" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#warnhandler"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>warnHandler</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>2.4.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Function</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>默认值</strong>：<code>undefined</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">warnHandler</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">msg</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">trace</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// `trace` 是组件的继承关系追踪</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p>为 Vue 的运行时警告赋予一个自定义处理函数。注意这只会在开发者环境下生效，在生产环境下它会被忽略。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-ignoredelements" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#ignoredelements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>ignoredElements</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Array&lt;string | RegExp&gt;</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>默认值</strong>：<code>[]</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">ignoredElements</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-s">'my-custom-web-component'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">'another-web-component'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// 用一个 `RegExp` 忽略所有“ion-”开头的元素</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// 仅在 2.5+ 支持</span>
  <span class="pl-pds">/<span class="pl-cce">^</span>ion-/</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span></pre></div>
<p>须使 Vue 忽略在 Vue 之外的自定义元素 (e.g. 使用了 Web Components APIs)。否则，它会假设你忘记注册全局组件或者拼错了组件名称，从而抛出一个关于 <code>Unknown custom element</code> 的警告。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-keycodes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#keycodes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>keyCodes</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>{ [key: string]: number | Array&lt;number&gt; }</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>默认值</strong>：<code>{}</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">config</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">keyCodes</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">v</span>: <span class="pl-c1">86</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">f1</span>: <span class="pl-c1">112</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// camelCase 不可用</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">mediaPlayPause</span>: <span class="pl-c1">179</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// 取而代之的是 kebab-case 且用双引号括起来</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"media-play-pause"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">179</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">up</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">38</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">87</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">input</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span>="<span class="pl-s">text</span>" <span class="pl-c1">@keyup.media-play-pause</span>="<span class="pl-s">method</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p>给 <code>v-on</code> 自定义键位别名。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-performance" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#performance"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>performance</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>2.2.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>boolean</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>默认值</strong>：<code>false (自 2.2.3 起)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>设置为 <code>true</code> 以在浏览器开发工具的性能/时间线面板中启用对组件初始化、编译、渲染和打补丁的性能追踪。只适用于开发模式和支持 <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Performance/mark" rel="nofollow"><code>performance.mark</code></a> API 的浏览器上。
 </p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-productiontip" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#productiontip"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>productionTip</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>2.2.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>boolean</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>默认值</strong>：<code>true</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>设置为 <code>false</code> 以阻止 vue 在启动时生成生产提示。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-全局-api" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#全局-api"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>全局 API</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-vueextend-options-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vueextend-options-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Vue.extend( options )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{Object} options</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>使用基础 Vue 构造器，创建一个“子类”。参数是一个包含组件选项的对象。</p>
<p><code>data</code> 选项是特例，需要注意 - 在 <code>Vue.extend()</code> 中它必须是函数</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span>="<span class="pl-s">mount-point</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-c">// 创建构造器</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-v">Profile</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">extend</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">template</span>: <span class="pl-s">'&lt;p&gt;{{firstName}} {{lastName}} aka {{alias}}&lt;/p&gt;'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-en">data</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">firstName</span>: <span class="pl-s">'Walter'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">lastName</span>: <span class="pl-s">'White'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">alias</span>: <span class="pl-s">'Heisenberg'</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-c">// 创建 Profile 实例，并挂载到一个元素上。</span>
<span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Profile</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$mount</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'#mount-point'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p>结果如下：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>Walter White aka Heisenberg<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components.html">组件</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vuenexttick-callback-context-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vuenexttick-callback-context-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Vue.nextTick( [callback, context] )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{Function} [callback]</code></li>
<li><code>{Object} [context]</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>在下次 DOM 更新循环结束之后执行延迟回调。在修改数据之后立即使用这个方法，获取更新后的 DOM。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-c">// 修改数据</span>
<span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">msg</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'Hello'</span>
<span class="pl-c">// DOM 还没有更新</span>
<span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">nextTick</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// DOM 更新了</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 作为一个 Promise 使用 (2.1.0 起新增，详见接下来的提示)</span>
<span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">nextTick</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">then</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// DOM 更新了</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p> &gt; 2.1.0 起新增：如果没有提供回调且在支持 Promise 的环境中，则返回一个 Promise。请注意 Vue 不自带 Promise 的 polyfill，所以如果你的目标浏览器不原生支持 Promise (IE：你们都看我干嘛)，你得自己提供 polyfill。</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/reactivity.html#%E5%BC%82%E6%AD%A5%E6%9B%B4%E6%96%B0%E9%98%9F%E5%88%97">异步更新队列</a></li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vueset-target-propertynameindex-value-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vueset-target-propertynameindex-value-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Vue.set( target, propertyName/index, value )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{Object | Array} target</code></li>
<li><code>{string | number} propertyName/index</code></li>
<li><code>{any} value</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>返回值</strong>：设置的值。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>向响应式对象中添加一个 property，并确保这个新 property 同样是响应式的，且触发视图更新。它必须用于向响应式对象上添加新 property，因为 Vue 无法探测普通的新增 property (比如 <code>this.myObject.newProperty = 'hi'</code>)</p>
<p>注意对象不能是 Vue 实例，或者 Vue 实例的根数据对象。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vuedelete-target-propertynameindex-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vuedelete-target-propertynameindex-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Vue.delete( target, propertyName/index )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{Object | Array} target</code></li>
<li><code>{string | number} propertyName/index</code></li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p>仅在 2.2.0+ 版本中支持 Array + index 用法。</p>
</blockquote>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>删除对象的 property。如果对象是响应式的，确保删除能触发更新视图。这个方法主要用于避开 Vue 不能检测到 property 被删除的限制，但是你应该很少会使用它。</p>
<blockquote>
<p>在 2.2.0+ 中同样支持在数组上工作。</p>
</blockquote>
</li>
</ul>
<p> </p><p>目标对象不能是一个 Vue 实例或 Vue 实例的根数据对象。</p><p></p>
<ul>
<li><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/reactivity.html">深入响应式原理</a></li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vuedirective-id-definition-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vuedirective-id-definition-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Vue.directive( id, [definition] )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{string} id</code></li>
<li><code>{Function | Object} [definition]</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>注册或获取全局指令。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-c">// 注册</span>
<span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">directive</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-directive'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">bind</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-en">inserted</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-en">update</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-en">componentUpdated</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-en">unbind</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 注册 (指令函数)</span>
<span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">directive</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-directive'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// 这里将会被 `bind` 和 `update` 调用</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// getter，返回已注册的指令</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">myDirective</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">directive</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-directive'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/custom-directive.html">自定义指令</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vuefilter-id-definition-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vuefilter-id-definition-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Vue.filter( id, [definition] )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{string} id</code></li>
<li><code>{Function} [definition]</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>注册或获取全局过滤器。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-c">// 注册</span>
<span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">filter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-filter'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// 返回处理后的值</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// getter，返回已注册的过滤器</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">myFilter</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">filter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-filter'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/filters.html">过滤器</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vuecomponent-id-definition-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vuecomponent-id-definition-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Vue.component( id, [definition] )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{string} id</code></li>
<li><code>{Function | Object} [definition]</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>注册或获取全局组件。注册还会自动使用给定的 <code>id</code> 设置组件的名称</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-c">// 注册组件，传入一个扩展过的构造器</span>
<span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">component</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-component'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">extend</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c">/* ... */</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 注册组件，传入一个选项对象 (自动调用 Vue.extend)</span>
<span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">component</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-component'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c">/* ... */</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 获取注册的组件 (始终返回构造器)</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-v">MyComponent</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">component</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-component'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components.html">组件</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vueuse-plugin-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vueuse-plugin-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Vue.use( plugin )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{Object | Function} plugin</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>安装 Vue.js 插件。如果插件是一个对象，必须提供 <code>install</code> 方法。如果插件是一个函数，它会被作为 install 方法。install 方法调用时，会将 Vue 作为参数传入。</p>
<p>该方法需要在调用 <code>new Vue()</code> 之前被调用。</p>
<p>当 install 方法被同一个插件多次调用，插件将只会被安装一次。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/plugins.html">插件</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vuemixin-mixin-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vuemixin-mixin-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Vue.mixin( mixin )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{Object} mixin</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>全局注册一个混入，影响注册之后所有创建的每个 Vue 实例。插件作者可以使用混入，向组件注入自定义的行为。<strong>不推荐在应用代码中使用</strong>。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/mixins.html#%E5%85%A8%E5%B1%80%E6%B7%B7%E5%85%A5">全局混入</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vuecompile-template-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vuecompile-template-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Vue.compile( template )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{string} template</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>将一个模板字符串编译成 render 函数。<strong>只在完整版时可用</strong>。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">res</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">compile</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'&lt;div&gt;&lt;span&gt;{{ msg }}&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">data</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">msg</span>: <span class="pl-s">'hello'</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">render</span>: <span class="pl-s1">res</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">render</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">staticRenderFns</span>: <span class="pl-s1">res</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">staticRenderFns</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/render-function.html">渲染函数</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vueobservable-object-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vueobservable-object-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Vue.observable( object )</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>2.6.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{Object} object</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>让一个对象可响应。Vue 内部会用它来处理 <code>data</code> 函数返回的对象。</p>
<p>返回的对象可以直接用于<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/render-function.html">渲染函数</a>和<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/computed.html">计算属性</a>内，并且会在发生变更时触发相应的更新。也可以作为最小化的跨组件状态存储器，用于简单的场景：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">state</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">observable</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">count</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">Demo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">render</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">h</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">h</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'button'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">on</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-en">click</span>: <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">state</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">count</span><span class="pl-c1">++</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">`count is: <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">state</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">count</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p>在 Vue 2.x 中，被传入的对象会直接被 `Vue.observable` 变更，所以如[这里展示的](../guide/instance.html#数据与方法)，它和被返回的对象是同一个对象。在 Vue 3.x 中，则会返回一个可响应的代理，而对源对象直接进行变更仍然是不可响应的。因此，为了向前兼容，我们推荐始终操作使用 `Vue.observable` 返回的对象，而不是传入源对象。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/reactivity.html">深入响应式原理</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vueversion" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vueversion"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Vue.version</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>细节</strong>：提供字符串形式的 Vue 安装版本号。这对社区的插件和组件来说非常有用，你可以根据不同的版本号采取不同的策略。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">version</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Number</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">version</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">split</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'.'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">version</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// Vue v2.x.x</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">version</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// Vue v1.x.x</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// Unsupported versions of Vue</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-选项--数据" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#选项--数据"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>选项 / 数据</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-data" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#data"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>data</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Object | Function</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>限制</strong>：组件的定义只接受 <code>function</code>。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>Vue 实例的数据对象。Vue 将会递归将 data 的 property 转换为 getter/setter，从而让 data 的 property 能够响应数据变化。<strong>对象必须是纯粹的对象 (含有零个或多个的 key/value 对)</strong>：浏览器 API 创建的原生对象，原型上的 property 会被忽略。大概来说，data 应该只能是数据 - 不推荐观察拥有状态行为的对象。</p>
<p>一旦观察过，你就无法在根数据对象上添加响应式 property。因此推荐在创建实例之前，就声明所有的根级响应式 property。</p>
<p>实例创建之后，可以通过 <code>vm.$data</code> 访问原始数据对象。Vue 实例也代理了 data 对象上所有的 property，因此访问 <code>vm.a</code> 等价于访问 <code>vm.$data.a</code>。</p>
<p>以 <code>_</code> 或 <code>$</code> 开头的 property <strong>不会</strong>被 Vue 实例代理，因为它们可能和 Vue 内置的 property、API 方法冲突。你可以使用例如 <code>vm.$data._property</code> 的方式访问这些 property。</p>
<p>当一个<strong>组件</strong>被定义，<code>data</code> 必须声明为返回一个初始数据对象的函数，因为组件可能被用来创建多个实例。如果 <code>data</code> 仍然是一个纯粹的对象，则所有的实例将<strong>共享引用</strong>同一个数据对象！通过提供 <code>data</code> 函数，每次创建一个新实例后，我们能够调用 <code>data</code> 函数，从而返回初始数据的一个全新副本数据对象。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>如果需要，可以通过将 <code>vm.$data</code> 传入 <code>JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(...))</code> 得到深拷贝的原始数据对象。</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">data</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">a</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 直接创建一个实例</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">vm</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">data</span>: <span class="pl-s1">data</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">a</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; 1</span>
<span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">$data</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s1">data</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; true</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Vue.extend() 中 data 必须是函数</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-v">Component</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">extend</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">data</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">a</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p>注意，如果你为 <code>data</code> property 使用了箭头函数，则 <code>this</code> 不会指向这个组件的实例，不过你仍然可以将其实例作为函数的第一个参数来访问。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre>data: <span class="pl-s1">vm</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">a</span>: <span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">myProp</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/reactivity.html">深入响应式原理</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-props" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#props"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>props</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Array&lt;string&gt; | Object</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>props 可以是数组或对象，用于接收来自父组件的数据。props 可以是简单的数组，或者使用对象作为替代，对象允许配置高级选项，如类型检测、自定义验证和设置默认值。</p>
<p>你可以基于对象的语法使用以下选项：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>type</code>：可以是下列原生构造函数中的一种：<code>String</code>、<code>Number</code>、<code>Boolean</code>、<code>Array</code>、<code>Object</code>、<code>Date</code>、<code>Function</code>、<code>Symbol</code>、任何自定义构造函数、或上述内容组成的数组。会检查一个 prop 是否是给定的类型，否则抛出警告。Prop 类型的<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-props.html#Prop-%E7%B1%BB%E5%9E%8B">更多信息在此</a>。</li>
<li><code>default</code>：<code>any</code>
为该 prop 指定一个默认值。如果该 prop 没有被传入，则换做用这个值。对象或数组的默认值必须从一个工厂函数返回。</li>
<li><code>required</code>：<code>Boolean</code>
定义该 prop 是否是必填项。在非生产环境中，如果这个值为 truthy 且该 prop 没有被传入的，则一个控制台警告将会被抛出。</li>
<li><code>validator</code>：<code>Function</code>
自定义验证函数会将该 prop 的值作为唯一的参数代入。在非生产环境下，如果该函数返回一个 falsy 的值 (也就是验证失败)，一个控制台警告将会被抛出。你可以在<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-props.html#Prop-%E9%AA%8C%E8%AF%81">这里</a>查阅更多 prop 验证的相关信息。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-c">// 简单语法</span>
<span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">component</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'props-demo-simple'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">props</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'size'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'myMessage'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 对象语法，提供验证</span>
<span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">component</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'props-demo-advanced'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">props</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// 检测类型</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">height</span>: <span class="pl-v">Number</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// 检测类型 + 其他验证</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">age</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-v">Number</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">default</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">required</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-en">validator</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span> &gt;= <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-props.html">Props</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-propsdata" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#propsdata"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>propsData</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>{ [key: string]: any }</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>限制</strong>：只用于 <code>new</code> 创建的实例中。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>创建实例时传递 props。主要作用是方便测试。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-v">Comp</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">extend</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">props</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'msg'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">template</span>: <span class="pl-s">'&lt;div&gt;{{ msg }}&lt;/div&gt;'</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">vm</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Comp</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">propsData</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">msg</span>: <span class="pl-s">'hello'</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-computed" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#computed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>computed</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>{ [key: string]: Function | { get: Function, set: Function } }</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>计算属性将被混入到 Vue 实例中。所有 getter 和 setter 的 this 上下文自动地绑定为 Vue 实例。</p>
<p>注意如果你为一个计算属性使用了箭头函数，则 <code>this</code> 不会指向这个组件的实例，不过你仍然可以将其实例作为函数的第一个参数来访问。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre>computed: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">aDouble</span>: <span class="pl-s1">vm</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">a</span> * <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p> 计算属性的结果会被缓存，除非依赖的响应式 property 变化才会重新计算。注意，如果某个依赖 (比如非响应式 property) 在该实例范畴之外，则计算属性是<strong>不会</strong>被更新的。</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">vm</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">data</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">a</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">computed</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// 仅读取</span>
    <span class="pl-en">aDouble</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">a</span> * <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// 读取和设置</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">aPlus</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-en">get</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-en">set</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">v</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">v</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">aPlus</span>   <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; 2</span>
<span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">aPlus</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span>
<span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">a</span>       <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; 2</span>
<span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">aDouble</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; 4</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/computed.html">计算属性</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-methods" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#methods"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>methods</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>{ [key: string]: Function }</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>methods 将被混入到 Vue 实例中。可以直接通过 VM 实例访问这些方法，或者在指令表达式中使用。方法中的 <code>this</code> 自动绑定为 Vue 实例。</p>
<p>注意，**不应该使用箭头函数来定义 method 函数** (例如 `plus: () =&gt; this.a++`)。理由是箭头函数绑定了父级作用域的上下文，所以 `this` 将不会按照期望指向 Vue 实例，`this.a` 将是 undefined。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">vm</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">data</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">a</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">methods</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-en">plus</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">a</span><span class="pl-c1">++</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">plus</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">a</span> <span class="pl-c">// 2</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/events.html">事件处理器</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-watch" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#watch"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>watch</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>{ [key: string]: string | Function | Object | Array }</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>一个对象，键是需要观察的表达式，值是对应回调函数。值也可以是方法名，或者包含选项的对象。Vue 实例将会在实例化时调用 <code>$watch()</code>，遍历 watch 对象的每一个 property。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">vm</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">data</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">a</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">b</span>: <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">c</span>: <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">d</span>: <span class="pl-c1">4</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">e</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">f</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">g</span>: <span class="pl-c1">5</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">watch</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-en">a</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">val</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">oldVal</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'new: %s, old: %s'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">val</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">oldVal</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// 方法名</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">b</span>: <span class="pl-s">'someMethod'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// 该回调会在任何被侦听的对象的 property 改变时被调用，不论其被嵌套多深</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">c</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-en">handler</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">val</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">oldVal</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c">/* ... */</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">deep</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// 该回调将会在侦听开始之后被立即调用</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">d</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">handler</span>: <span class="pl-s">'someMethod'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">immediate</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// 你可以传入回调数组，它们会被逐一调用</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">e</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
      <span class="pl-s">'handle1'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">handle2</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">val</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">oldVal</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c">/* ... */</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-en">handler</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">handle3</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">val</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">oldVal</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c">/* ... */</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c">/* ... */</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// watch vm.e.f's value: {g: 5}</span>
    <span class="pl-s">'e.f'</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">val</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">oldVal</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c">/* ... */</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; new: 2, old: 1</span></pre></div>
<p>注意，**不应该使用箭头函数来定义 watcher 函数** (例如 `searchQuery: newValue =&gt; this.updateAutocomplete(newValue)`)。理由是箭头函数绑定了父级作用域的上下文，所以 `this` 将不会按照期望指向 Vue 实例，`this.updateAutocomplete` 将是 undefined。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="#vm-watch">实例方法 / 数据 - vm.$watch</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-选项--dom" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#选项--dom"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>选项 / DOM</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-el" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#el"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>el</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>string | Element</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>限制</strong>：只在用 <code>new</code> 创建实例时生效。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>提供一个在页面上已存在的 DOM 元素作为 Vue 实例的挂载目标。可以是 CSS 选择器，也可以是一个 HTMLElement 实例。</p>
<p>在实例挂载之后，元素可以用 <code>vm.$el</code> 访问。</p>
<p>如果在实例化时存在这个选项，实例将立即进入编译过程，否则，需要显式调用 <code>vm.$mount()</code> 手动开启编译。</p>
<p> 提供的元素只能作为挂载点。不同于 Vue 1.x，所有的挂载元素会被 Vue 生成的 DOM 替换。因此不推荐挂载 root 实例到 `` 或者 `` 上。</p>
<p>如果 `render` 函数和 `template` property 都不存在，挂载 DOM 元素的 HTML 会被提取出来用作模板，此时，必须使用 Runtime + Compiler 构建的 Vue 库。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/instance.html#%E7%94%9F%E5%91%BD%E5%91%A8%E6%9C%9F%E5%9B%BE%E7%A4%BA">生命周期图示</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/installation.html#%E8%BF%90%E8%A1%8C%E6%97%B6-%E7%BC%96%E8%AF%91%E5%99%A8-vs-%E5%8F%AA%E5%8C%85%E5%90%AB%E8%BF%90%E8%A1%8C%E6%97%B6">运行时 + 编译器 vs. 只包含运行时</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-template" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#template"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>template</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>string</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>一个字符串模板作为 Vue 实例的标识使用。模板将会<strong>替换</strong>挂载的元素。挂载元素的内容都将被忽略，除非模板的内容有分发插槽。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p> 如果值以 <code>#</code> 开始，则它将被用作选择符，并使用匹配元素的 innerHTML 作为模板。常用的技巧是用 <code>&lt;script type="x-template"&gt;</code> 包含模板。</p>
<p> </p><p>出于安全考虑，你应该只使用你信任的 Vue 模板。避免使用其他人生成的内容作为你的模板。</p><p></p>
<p> </p><p>如果 Vue 选项中包含渲染函数，该模板将被忽略。</p><p></p>
<ul>
<li><strong>参考</strong>：
<ul>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/instance.html#%E7%94%9F%E5%91%BD%E5%91%A8%E6%9C%9F%E5%9B%BE%E7%A4%BA">生命周期图示</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components.html#%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87%E6%8F%92%E6%A7%BD%E5%88%86%E5%8F%91%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9">通过插槽分发内容</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-render" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#render"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>render</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>(createElement: () =&gt; VNode) =&gt; VNode</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>   字符串模板的代替方案，允许你发挥 JavaScript 最大的编程能力。该渲染函数接收一个 <code>createElement</code> 方法作为第一个参数用来创建 <code>VNode</code>。</p>
<pre><code>如果组件是一个函数组件，渲染函数还会接收一个额外的 `context` 参数，为没有实例的函数组件提供上下文信息。
</code></pre>
<p>   </p><p>Vue 选项中的 <code>render</code> 函数若存在，则 Vue 构造函数不会从 <code>template</code> 选项或通过 <code>el</code> 选项指定的挂载元素中提取出的 HTML 模板编译渲染函数。</p><p></p>
<ul>
<li><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/render-function.html">渲染函数</a></li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-rendererror" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#rendererror"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>renderError</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>2.2.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>(createElement: () =&gt; VNode, error: Error) =&gt; VNode</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p><strong>只在开发者环境下工作。</strong></p>
<p>当 <code>render</code> 函数遭遇错误时，提供另外一种渲染输出。其错误将会作为第二个参数传递到 <code>renderError</code>。这个功能配合 hot-reload 非常实用。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">render</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">h</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">throw</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Error</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'oops'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-en">renderError</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">h</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">err</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">h</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'pre'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">style</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">color</span>: <span class="pl-s">'red'</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">err</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">stack</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$mount</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'#app'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/render-function.html">渲染函数</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-选项--生命周期钩子" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#选项--生命周期钩子"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>选项 / 生命周期钩子</h2>
<p>所有的生命周期钩子自动绑定 `this` 上下文到实例中，因此你可以访问数据，对 property 和方法进行运算。这意味着**你不能使用箭头函数来定义一个生命周期方法** (例如 `created: () =&gt; this.fetchTodos()`)。这是因为箭头函数绑定了父上下文，因此 `this` 与你期待的 Vue 实例不同，`this.fetchTodos` 的行为未定义。</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-beforecreate" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#beforecreate"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>beforeCreate</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Function</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>在实例初始化之后，数据观测 (data observer) 和 event/watcher 事件配置之前被调用。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/instance.html#%E7%94%9F%E5%91%BD%E5%91%A8%E6%9C%9F%E5%9B%BE%E7%A4%BA">生命周期图示</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-created" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#created"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>created</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Function</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>在实例创建完成后被立即调用。在这一步，实例已完成以下的配置：数据观测 (data observer)，property 和方法的运算，watch/event 事件回调。然而，挂载阶段还没开始，<code>$el</code> property 目前尚不可用。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/instance.html#%E7%94%9F%E5%91%BD%E5%91%A8%E6%9C%9F%E5%9B%BE%E7%A4%BA">生命周期图示</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-beforemount" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#beforemount"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>beforeMount</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Function</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>在挂载开始之前被调用：相关的 <code>render</code> 函数首次被调用。</p>
<p><strong>该钩子在服务器端渲染期间不被调用。</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/instance.html#%E7%94%9F%E5%91%BD%E5%91%A8%E6%9C%9F%E5%9B%BE%E7%A4%BA">生命周期图示</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-mounted" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#mounted"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>mounted</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Function</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>实例被挂载后调用，这时 <code>el</code> 被新创建的 <code>vm.$el</code> 替换了。如果根实例挂载到了一个文档内的元素上，当 <code>mounted</code> 被调用时 <code>vm.$el</code> 也在文档内。</p>
<p>注意 <code>mounted</code> <strong>不会</strong>保证所有的子组件也都一起被挂载。如果你希望等到整个视图都渲染完毕，可以在 <code>mounted</code> 内部使用 <a href="#vm-nextTick">vm.$nextTick</a>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre>mounted: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$nextTick</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// Code that will run only after the</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// entire view has been rendered</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p><strong>该钩子在服务器端渲染期间不被调用。</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/instance.html#%E7%94%9F%E5%91%BD%E5%91%A8%E6%9C%9F%E5%9B%BE%E7%A4%BA">生命周期图示</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-beforeupdate" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#beforeupdate"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>beforeUpdate</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Function</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>数据更新时调用，发生在虚拟 DOM 打补丁之前。这里适合在更新之前访问现有的 DOM，比如手动移除已添加的事件监听器。</p>
<p><strong>该钩子在服务器端渲染期间不被调用，因为只有初次渲染会在服务端进行。</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/instance.html#%E7%94%9F%E5%91%BD%E5%91%A8%E6%9C%9F%E5%9B%BE%E7%A4%BA">生命周期图示</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
