<h3><a id="user-content-updated" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#updated"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>updated</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Function</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>由于数据更改导致的虚拟 DOM 重新渲染和打补丁，在这之后会调用该钩子。</p>
<p>当这个钩子被调用时，组件 DOM 已经更新，所以你现在可以执行依赖于 DOM 的操作。然而在大多数情况下，你应该避免在此期间更改状态。如果要相应状态改变，通常最好使用<a href="#computed">计算属性</a>或 <a href="#watch">watcher</a> 取而代之。</p>
<p>注意 <code>updated</code> <strong>不会</strong>保证所有的子组件也都一起被重绘。如果你希望等到整个视图都重绘完毕，可以在 <code>updated</code> 里使用 <a href="#vm-nextTick">vm.$nextTick</a>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre>updated: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$nextTick</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// Code that will run only after the</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// entire view has been re-rendered</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p><strong>该钩子在服务器端渲染期间不被调用。</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/instance.html#%E7%94%9F%E5%91%BD%E5%91%A8%E6%9C%9F%E5%9B%BE%E7%A4%BA">生命周期图示</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-activated" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#activated"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>activated</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Function</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>被 keep-alive 缓存的组件激活时调用。</p>
<p><strong>该钩子在服务器端渲染期间不被调用。</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#keep-alive">构建组件 - keep-alive</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-dynamic-async.html#%E5%9C%A8%E5%8A%A8%E6%80%81%E7%BB%84%E4%BB%B6%E4%B8%8A%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8-keep-alive">动态组件 - keep-alive</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-deactivated" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#deactivated"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>deactivated</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Function</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>被 keep-alive 缓存的组件停用时调用。</p>
<p><strong>该钩子在服务器端渲染期间不被调用。</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#keep-alive">构建组件 - keep-alive</a></li>

</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-beforedestroy" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#beforedestroy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>beforeDestroy</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Function</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>实例销毁之前调用。在这一步，实例仍然完全可用。</p>
<p><strong>该钩子在服务器端渲染期间不被调用。</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/instance.html#%E7%94%9F%E5%91%BD%E5%91%A8%E6%9C%9F%E5%9B%BE%E7%A4%BA">生命周期图示</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-destroyed" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#destroyed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>destroyed</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Function</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>实例销毁后调用。该钩子被调用后，对应 Vue 实例的所有指令都被解绑，所有的事件监听器被移除，所有的子实例也都被销毁。</p>
<p><strong>该钩子在服务器端渲染期间不被调用。</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/instance.html#%E7%94%9F%E5%91%BD%E5%91%A8%E6%9C%9F%E5%9B%BE%E7%A4%BA">生命周期图示</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-errorcaptured" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#errorcaptured"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>errorCaptured</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>2.5.0+ 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>(err: Error, vm: Component, info: string) =&gt; ?boolean</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>当捕获一个来自子孙组件的错误时被调用。此钩子会收到三个参数：错误对象、发生错误的组件实例以及一个包含错误来源信息的字符串。此钩子可以返回 <code>false</code> 以阻止该错误继续向上传播。</p>
<p>你可以在此钩子中修改组件的状态。因此在捕获错误时，在模板或渲染函数中有一个条件判断来绕过其它内容就很重要；不然该组件可能会进入一个无限的渲染循环。</p>
<p><strong>错误传播规则</strong></p>
</li>
</ul>
<p> - 默认情况下，如果全局的 <code>config.errorHandler</code> 被定义，所有的错误仍会发送它，因此这些错误仍然会向单一的分析服务的地方进行汇报。</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>如果一个组件的继承或父级从属链路中存在多个 <code>errorCaptured</code> 钩子，则它们将会被相同的错误逐个唤起。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>如果此 <code>errorCaptured</code> 钩子自身抛出了一个错误，则这个新错误和原本被捕获的错误都会发送给全局的 <code>config.errorHandler</code>。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>一个 <code>errorCaptured</code> 钩子能够返回 <code>false</code> 以阻止错误继续向上传播。本质上是说“这个错误已经被搞定了且应该被忽略”。它会阻止其它任何会被这个错误唤起的 <code>errorCaptured</code> 钩子和全局的 <code>config.errorHandler</code>。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-选项--资源" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#选项--资源"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>选项 / 资源</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-directives" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#directives"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>directives</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Object</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>包含 Vue 实例可用指令的哈希表。</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/custom-directive.html">自定义指令</a></li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-filters" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#filters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>filters</h3>

</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-components" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#components"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>components</h3>

<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>

<p>包含 Vue 实例可用组件的哈希表。</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components.html">组件</a></li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-选项--组合" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#选项--组合"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>选项 / 组合</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-parent" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#parent"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>parent</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Vue instance</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>指定已创建的实例之父实例，在两者之间建立父子关系。子实例可以用 <code>this.$parent</code> 访问父实例，子实例被推入父实例的 <code>$children</code> 数组中。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p> </p><p>节制地使用 <code>$parent</code> 和 <code>$children</code> - 它们的主要目的是作为访问组件的应急方法。更推荐用 props 和 events 实现父子组件通信</p><p></p>
<h3><a id="user-content-mixins" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#mixins"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>mixins</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Array&lt;Object&gt;</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p><code>mixins</code> 选项接收一个混入对象的数组。这些混入对象可以像正常的实例对象一样包含实例选项，这些选项将会被合并到最终的选项中，使用的是和 <code>Vue.extend()</code> 一样的选项合并逻辑。也就是说，如果你的混入包含一个 created 钩子，而创建组件本身也有一个，那么两个函数都会被调用。</p>
<p>Mixin 钩子按照传入顺序依次调用，并在调用组件自身的钩子之前被调用。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">mixin</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">created</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">vm</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">created</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">mixins</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">mixin</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-c">// =&gt; 1</span>
<span class="pl-c">// =&gt; 2</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/mixins.html">混入</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-extends" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#extends"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>extends</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Object | Function</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>允许声明扩展另一个组件 (可以是一个简单的选项对象或构造函数)，而无需使用 <code>Vue.extend</code>。这主要是为了便于扩展单文件组件。</p>
<p>这和 <code>mixins</code> 类似。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-v">CompA</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> ... <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 在没有调用 `Vue.extend` 时候继承 CompA</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-v">CompB</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">extends</span>: <span class="pl-v">CompA</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  ...
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-provide--inject" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#provide--inject"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>provide / inject</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>2.2.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>provide</strong>：<code>Object | () =&gt; Object</code></li>
<li><strong>inject</strong>：<code>Array&lt;string&gt; | { [key: string]: string | Symbol | Object }</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>`provide` 和 `inject` 主要在开发高阶插件/组件库时使用。并不推荐用于普通应用程序代码中。</p>
<p>这对选项需要一起使用，以允许一个祖先组件向其所有子孙后代注入一个依赖，不论组件层次有多深，并在其上下游关系成立的时间里始终生效。如果你熟悉 React，这与 React 的上下文特性很相似。</p>
<p><code>provide</code> 选项应该是一个对象或返回一个对象的函数。该对象包含可注入其子孙的 property。在该对象中你可以使用 ES2015 Symbols 作为 key，但是只在原生支持 <code>Symbol</code> 和 <code>Reflect.ownKeys</code> 的环境下可工作。</p>
<p><code>inject</code> 选项应该是：</p>
<ul>
<li>一个字符串数组，或</li>
<li>一个对象，对象的 key 是本地的绑定名，value 是：
<ul>
<li>在可用的注入内容中搜索用的 key (字符串或 Symbol)，或</li>
<li>一个对象，该对象的：
<ul>
<li><code>from</code> property 是在可用的注入内容中搜索用的 key (字符串或 Symbol)</li>
<li><code>default</code> property 是降级情况下使用的 value</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p>提示：<code>provide</code> 和 <code>inject</code> 绑定并不是可响应的。这是刻意为之的。然而，如果你传入了一个可监听的对象，那么其对象的 property 还是可响应的。</p>
</blockquote>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-c">// 父级组件提供 'foo'</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-v">Provider</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">provide</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">foo</span>: <span class="pl-s">'bar'</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 子组件注入 'foo'</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-v">Child</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">inject</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-en">created</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; "bar"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p>利用 ES2015 Symbols、函数 <code>provide</code> 和对象 <code>inject</code>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">s</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Symbol</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">Provider</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">provide</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">s</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>: <span class="pl-s">'foo'</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">Child</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">inject</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> s <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>接下来 2 个例子只工作在 Vue 2.2.1 或更高版本。低于这个版本时，注入的值会在 <code>props</code> 和 <code>data</code> 初始化之后得到。</p>
</blockquote>
<p>使用一个注入的值作为一个 property 的默认值：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">Child</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">inject</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">props</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">bar</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-en">default</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">foo</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p>使用一个注入的值作为数据入口：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">Child</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">inject</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-en">data</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">bar</span>: <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">foo</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>在 2.5.0+ 的注入可以通过设置默认值使其变成可选项：</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">Child</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">inject</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">foo</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">default</span>: <span class="pl-s">'foo'</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p>如果它需要从一个不同名字的 property 注入，则使用 <code>from</code> 来表示其源 property：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">Child</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">inject</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">foo</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">from</span>: <span class="pl-s">'bar'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">default</span>: <span class="pl-s">'foo'</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p>与 prop 的默认值类似，你需要对非原始值使用一个工厂方法：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">Child</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">inject</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">foo</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">from</span>: <span class="pl-s">'bar'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-en">default</span>: <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-选项--其它" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#选项--其它"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>选项 / 其它</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-name" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#name"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>name</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>string</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>限制</strong>：只有作为组件选项时起作用。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>允许组件模板递归地调用自身。注意，组件在全局用 <code>Vue.component()</code> 注册时，全局 ID 自动作为组件的 name。</p>
<p>指定 <code>name</code> 选项的另一个好处是便于调试。有名字的组件有更友好的警告信息。另外，当在有 <a href="https://github.com/vuejs/vue-devtools">vue-devtools</a>，未命名组件将显示成 <code>&lt;AnonymousComponent&gt;</code>，这很没有语义。通过提供 <code>name</code> 选项，可以获得更有语义信息的组件树。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-delimiters" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#delimiters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>delimiters</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Array&lt;string&gt;</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>默认值</strong>：<code>{% raw %}["{{", "}}"]{% endraw %}</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>限制</strong>：这个选项只在完整构建版本中的浏览器内编译时可用。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>改变纯文本插入分隔符。</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">delimiters</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'${'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'}'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 分隔符变成了 ES6 模板字符串的风格</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-functional" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#functional"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>functional</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>boolean</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>使组件无状态 (没有 <code>data</code>) 和无实例 (没有 <code>this</code> 上下文)。他们用一个简单的 <code>render</code> 函数返回虚拟节点使它们渲染的代价更小。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/render-function.html#%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0%E5%BC%8F%E7%BB%84%E4%BB%B6">函数式组件</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-model" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#model"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>model</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>2.2.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>{ prop?: string, event?: string }</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>允许一个自定义组件在使用 <code>v-model</code> 时定制 prop 和 event。默认情况下，一个组件上的 <code>v-model</code> 会把 <code>value</code> 用作 prop 且把 <code>input</code> 用作 event，但是一些输入类型比如单选框和复选框按钮可能想使用 <code>value</code> prop 来达到不同的目的。使用 <code>model</code> 选项可以回避这些情况产生的冲突。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Example</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">component</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-checkbox'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">model</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">prop</span>: <span class="pl-s">'checked'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">event</span>: <span class="pl-s">'change'</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">props</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// this allows using the `value` prop for a different purpose</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">value</span>: <span class="pl-v">String</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// use `checked` as the prop which take the place of `value`</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">checked</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-v">Number</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">default</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">my-checkbox</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-model</span>="<span class="pl-s">foo</span>" <span class="pl-c1">value</span>="<span class="pl-s">some value</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">my-checkbox</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p>上述代码相当于：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">my-checkbox</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">:checked</span>="<span class="pl-s">foo</span>"
  <span class="pl-c1">@change</span>="<span class="pl-s">val =&gt; { foo = val }</span>"
  <span class="pl-c1">value</span>="<span class="pl-s">some value</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">my-checkbox</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-inheritattrs" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#inheritattrs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>inheritAttrs</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>2.4.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>boolean</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>默认值</strong>：<code>true</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>默认情况下父作用域的不被认作 props 的 attribute 绑定 (attribute bindings) 将会“回退”且作为普通的 HTML attribute 应用在子组件的根元素上。当撰写包裹一个目标元素或另一个组件的组件时，这可能不会总是符合预期行为。通过设置 <code>inheritAttrs</code> 到 <code>false</code>，这些默认行为将会被去掉。而通过 (同样是 2.4 新增的) 实例 property <code>$attrs</code> 可以让这些 attribute 生效，且可以通过 <code>v-bind</code> 显性的绑定到非根元素上。</p>
<p>注意：这个选项<strong>不影响</strong> <code>class</code> 和 <code>style</code> 绑定。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-comments" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#comments"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>comments</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>2.4.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>boolean</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>默认值</strong>：<code>false</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>限制</strong>：这个选项只在完整构建版本中的浏览器内编译时可用。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>当设为 <code>true</code> 时，将会保留且渲染模板中的 HTML 注释。默认行为是舍弃它们。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-实例-property" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#实例-property"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>实例 property</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmdata" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmdata"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$data</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Object</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>Vue 实例观察的数据对象。Vue 实例代理了对其 data 对象 property 的访问。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="#data">选项 / 数据 - data</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmprops" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmprops"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$props</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>2.2.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Object</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>当前组件接收到的 props 对象。Vue 实例代理了对其 props 对象 property 的访问。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmel" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmel"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$el</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Element</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>只读</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>Vue 实例使用的根 DOM 元素。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmoptions" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmoptions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$options</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Object</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>只读</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>用于当前 Vue 实例的初始化选项。需要在选项中包含自定义 property 时会有用处：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">customOption</span>: <span class="pl-s">'foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-en">created</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">$options</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">customOption</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; 'foo'</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmparent" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmparent"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$parent</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Vue instance</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>只读</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>父实例，如果当前实例有的话。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmroot" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmroot"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$root</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Vue instance</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>只读</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p> 当前组件树的根 Vue 实例。如果当前实例没有父实例，此实例将会是其自己。</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmchildren" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmchildren"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$children</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Array&lt;Vue instance&gt;</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>只读</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>当前实例的直接子组件。**需要注意 <code>$children</code> 并不保证顺序，也不是响应式的。**如果你发现自己正在尝试使用 <code>$children</code> 来进行数据绑定，考虑使用一个数组配合 <code>v-for</code> 来生成子组件，并且使用 Array 作为真正的来源。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmslots" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmslots"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$slots</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>{ [name: string]: ?Array&lt;VNode&gt; }</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>只读</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>响应性</strong>：否</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>用来访问被<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components.html#%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87%E6%8F%92%E6%A7%BD%E5%88%86%E5%8F%91%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9">插槽分发</a>的内容。每个<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-slots.html#%E5%85%B7%E5%90%8D%E6%8F%92%E6%A7%BD">具名插槽</a>有其相应的 property (例如：<code>v-slot:foo</code> 中的内容将会在 <code>vm.$slots.foo</code> 中被找到)。<code>default</code> property 包括了所有没有被包含在具名插槽中的节点，或 <code>v-slot:default</code> 的内容。</p>
<p>请注意插槽<strong>不是</strong>响应性的。如果你需要一个组件可以在被传入的数据发生变化时重渲染，我们建议改变策略，依赖诸如 <code>props</code> 或 <code>data</code> 等响应性实例选项。</p>
<p><strong>注意：</strong><code>v-slot:foo</code> 在 2.6 以上的版本才支持。对于之前的版本，你可以使用<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-slots.html#%E5%BA%9F%E5%BC%83%E4%BA%86%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95">废弃了的语法</a>。</p>
<p>在使用<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/render-function.html">渲染函数</a>书写一个组件时，访问 <code>vm.$slots</code> 最有帮助。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">blog-post</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">template</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-slot:header</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>About Me<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">template</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>Here's some page content, which will be included in vm.$slots.default, because it's not inside a named slot.<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">template</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-slot:footer</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>Copyright 2016 Evan You<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">template</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>If I have some content down here, it will also be included in vm.$slots.default.<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>.
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">blog-post</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">component</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'blog-post'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">render</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">createElement</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">header</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">$slots</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">header</span>
    <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">body</span>   <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">$slots</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">default</span>
    <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">footer</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">$slots</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">footer</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">createElement</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'div'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
      <span class="pl-s1">createElement</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'header'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">header</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-s1">createElement</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'main'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">body</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-s1">createElement</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'footer'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">footer</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#slot"><code>&lt;slot&gt;</code> 组件</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components.html#%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87%E6%8F%92%E6%A7%BD%E5%88%86%E5%8F%91%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9">通过插槽分发内容</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/render-function.html#%E6%8F%92%E6%A7%BD">渲染函数 - 插槽</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmscopedslots" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmscopedslots"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$scopedSlots</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>2.1.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>{ [name: string]: props =&gt; Array&lt;VNode&gt; | undefined }</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>只读</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>用来访问<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-slots.html#%E4%BD%9C%E7%94%A8%E5%9F%9F%E6%8F%92%E6%A7%BD">作用域插槽</a>。对于包括 <code>默认 slot</code> 在内的每一个插槽，该对象都包含一个返回相应 VNode 的函数。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p> <code>vm.$scopedSlots</code> 在使用<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/render-function.html">渲染函数</a>开发一个组件时特别有用。</p>
<p><strong>注意</strong>：从 2.6.0 开始，这个 property 有两个变化：</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p>作用域插槽函数现在保证返回一个 VNode 数组，除非在返回值无效的情况下返回 <code>undefined</code>。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>所有的 <code>$slots</code> 现在都会作为函数暴露在 <code>$scopedSlots</code> 中。如果你在使用渲染函数，不论当前插槽是否带有作用域，我们都推荐始终通过 <code>$scopedSlots</code> 访问它们。这不仅仅使得在未来添加作用域变得简单，也可以让你最终轻松迁移到所有插槽都是函数的 Vue 3。</p>
</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li><strong>参考</strong>：
<ul>
<li><a href="#slot"><code>&lt;slot&gt;</code> 组件</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-slots.html#%E4%BD%9C%E7%94%A8%E5%9F%9F%E6%8F%92%E6%A7%BD">作用域插槽</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/render-function.html#%E6%8F%92%E6%A7%BD">渲染函数 - 插槽</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmrefs" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmrefs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$refs</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>Object</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>只读</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>一个对象，持有注册过 <a href="#ref"><code>ref</code> attribute</a> 的所有 DOM 元素和组件实例。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-edge-cases.html#%E8%AE%BF%E9%97%AE%E5%AD%90%E7%BB%84%E4%BB%B6%E5%AE%9E%E4%BE%8B%E6%88%96%E5%AD%90%E5%85%83%E7%B4%A0">子组件 ref</a></li>
<li><a href="#ref">特殊 attribute - ref</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmisserver" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmisserver"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$isServer</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>boolean</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>只读</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>当前 Vue 实例是否运行于服务器。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/ssr.html">服务端渲染</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmattrs" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmattrs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$attrs</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>2.4.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>{ [key: string]: string }</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>只读</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>包含了父作用域中不作为 prop 被识别 (且获取) 的 attribute 绑定 (<code>class</code> 和 <code>style</code> 除外)。当一个组件没有声明任何 prop 时，这里会包含所有父作用域的绑定 (<code>class</code> 和 <code>style</code> 除外)，并且可以通过 <code>v-bind="$attrs"</code> 传入内部组件——在创建高级别的组件时非常有用。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmlisteners" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmlisteners"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$listeners</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>2.4.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>{ [key: string]: Function | Array&lt;Function&gt; }</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>只读</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>包含了父作用域中的 (不含 <code>.native</code> 修饰器的) <code>v-on</code> 事件监听器。它可以通过 <code>v-on="$listeners"</code> 传入内部组件——在创建更高层次的组件时非常有用。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-实例方法--数据" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#实例方法--数据"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>实例方法 / 数据</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmwatch-exporfn-callback-options-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmwatch-exporfn-callback-options-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$watch( expOrFn, callback, [options] )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{string | Function} expOrFn</code></li>
<li><code>{Function | Object} callback</code></li>
<li><code>{Object} [options]</code>
<ul>
<li><code>{boolean} deep</code></li>
<li><code>{boolean} immediate</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>返回值</strong>：<code>{Function} unwatch</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>观察 Vue 实例上的一个表达式或者一个函数计算结果的变化。回调函数得到的参数为新值和旧值。表达式只接受简单的键路径。对于更复杂的表达式，用一个函数取代。</p>
<p>注意：在变更 (不是替换) 对象或数组时，旧值将与新值相同，因为它们的引用指向同一个对象/数组。Vue 不会保留变更之前值的副本。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-c">// 键路径</span>
<span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$watch</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'a.b.c'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">newVal</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">oldVal</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// 做点什么</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 函数</span>
<span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$watch</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// 表达式 `this.a + this.b` 每次得出一个不同的结果时</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// 处理函数都会被调用。</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// 这就像监听一个未被定义的计算属性</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">b</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">newVal</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">oldVal</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// 做点什么</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p><code>vm.$watch</code> 返回一个取消观察函数，用来停止触发回调：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">unwatch</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$watch</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'a'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">cb</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-c">// 之后取消观察</span>
<span class="pl-s1">unwatch</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>选项：deep</strong></p>
<p>为了发现对象内部值的变化，可以在选项参数中指定 <code>deep: true</code>。注意监听数组的变更不需要这么做。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$watch</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'someObject'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">callback</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">deep</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">someObject</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">nestedValue</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">123</span>
<span class="pl-c">// callback is fired</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>选项：immediate</strong></p>
<p>在选项参数中指定 <code>immediate: true</code> 将立即以表达式的当前值触发回调：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$watch</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'a'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">callback</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">immediate</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-c">// 立即以 `a` 的当前值触发回调</span></pre></div>
<p>注意在带有 <code>immediate</code> 选项时，你不能在第一次回调时取消侦听给定的 property。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-c">// 这会导致报错</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">unwatch</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$watch</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">'value'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-en">doSomething</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">unwatch</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">immediate</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p>如果你仍然希望在回调内部调用一个取消侦听的函数，你应该先检查其函数的可用性：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">unwatch</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$watch</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">'value'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-en">doSomething</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">unwatch</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-s1">unwatch</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">immediate</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmset-target-propertynameindex-value-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmset-target-propertynameindex-value-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$set( target, propertyName/index, value )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{Object | Array} target</code></li>
<li><code>{string | number} propertyName/index</code></li>
<li><code>{any} value</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>返回值</strong>：设置的值。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>这是全局 <code>Vue.set</code> 的<strong>别名</strong>。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="#Vue-set">Vue.set</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmdelete-target-propertynameindex-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmdelete-target-propertynameindex-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$delete( target, propertyName/index )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{Object | Array} target</code></li>
<li><code>{string | number} propertyName/index</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>这是全局 <code>Vue.delete</code> 的<strong>别名</strong>。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="#Vue-delete">Vue.delete</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-实例方法--事件" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#实例方法--事件"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>实例方法 / 事件</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmon-event-callback-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmon-event-callback-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$on( event, callback )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{string | Array&lt;string&gt;} event</code> (数组只在 2.2.0+ 中支持)</li>
<li><code>{Function} callback</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>监听当前实例上的自定义事件。事件可以由 <code>vm.$emit</code> 触发。回调函数会接收所有传入事件触发函数的额外参数。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$on</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'test'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">msg</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">msg</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-s1">vm</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$emit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'test'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'hi'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-c">// =&gt; "hi"</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmonce-event-callback-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmonce-event-callback-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$once( event, callback )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{string} event</code></li>
<li><code>{Function} callback</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>监听一个自定义事件，但是只触发一次。一旦触发之后，监听器就会被移除。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmoff-event-callback-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmoff-event-callback-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$off( [event, callback] )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{string | Array&lt;string&gt;} event</code> (只在 2.2.2+ 支持数组)</li>
<li><code>{Function} [callback]</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>移除自定义事件监听器。</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>如果没有提供参数，则移除所有的事件监听器；</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>如果只提供了事件，则移除该事件所有的监听器；</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>如果同时提供了事件与回调，则只移除这个回调的监听器。</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmemit-eventname-args-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmemit-eventname-args-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$emit( eventName, [...args] )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{string} eventName</code></li>
<li><code>[...args]</code></li>
</ul>
<p>触发当前实例上的事件。附加参数都会传给监听器回调。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例：</strong></p>
<p>只配合一个事件名使用 <code>$emit</code>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">component</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'welcome-button'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">template</span>: <span class="pl-s">`</span>
<span class="pl-s">    &lt;button v-on:click="$emit('welcome')"&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s">      Click me to be welcomed</span>
<span class="pl-s">    &lt;/button&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s">  `</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span>="<span class="pl-s">emit-example-simple</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">welcome-button</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-on:welcome</span>="<span class="pl-s">sayHi</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">welcome-button</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">el</span>: <span class="pl-s">'#emit-example-simple'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">methods</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-en">sayHi</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-en">alert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Hi!'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p>{% raw %}</p>
<div id="user-content-emit-example-simple">
  
</div>
&lt;script&gt;
  Vue.component('welcome-button', {
    template: `
      
        Click me to be welcomed
      
    `
  })
  new Vue({
    el: '#emit-example-simple',
    methods: {
      sayHi: function () {
        alert('Hi!')
      }
    }
  })
&lt;/script&gt;
{% endraw %}
<p>配合额外的参数使用 <code>$emit</code>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">component</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'magic-eight-ball'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">data</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">possibleAdvice</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'Yes'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'No'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'Maybe'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">methods</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-en">giveAdvice</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">randomAdviceIndex</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Math</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">floor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-v">Math</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">random</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> * <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">possibleAdvice</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
      <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$emit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'give-advice'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">possibleAdvice</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">randomAdviceIndex</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">template</span>: <span class="pl-s">`</span>
<span class="pl-s">    &lt;button v-on:click="giveAdvice"&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s">      Click me for advice</span>
<span class="pl-s">    &lt;/button&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s">  `</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span>="<span class="pl-s">emit-example-argument</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">magic-eight-ball</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-on:give-advice</span>="<span class="pl-s">showAdvice</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">magic-eight-ball</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">el</span>: <span class="pl-s">'#emit-example-argument'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">methods</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-en">showAdvice</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">advice</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-en">alert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">advice</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p>{% raw %}</p>
<div id="user-content-emit-example-argument">
  
</div>
&lt;script&gt;
  Vue.component('magic-eight-ball', {
    data: function () {
      return {
        possibleAdvice: ['Yes', 'No', 'Maybe']
      }
    },
    methods: {
      giveAdvice: function () {
        var randomAdviceIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * this.possibleAdvice.length)
        this.$emit('give-advice', this.possibleAdvice[randomAdviceIndex])
      }
    },
    template: `
      
        Click me for advice
      
    `
  })
  new Vue({
    el: '#emit-example-argument',
    methods: {
      showAdvice: function (advice) {
        alert(advice)
      }
    }
  })
&lt;/script&gt;
{% endraw %}
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-实例方法--生命周期" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#实例方法--生命周期"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>实例方法 / 生命周期</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmmount-elementorselector-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmmount-elementorselector-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$mount( [elementOrSelector] )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{Element | string} [elementOrSelector]</code></li>
<li><code>{boolean} [hydrating]</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>返回值</strong>：<code>vm</code> - 实例自身</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>如果 Vue 实例在实例化时没有收到 el 选项，则它处于“未挂载”状态，没有关联的 DOM 元素。可以使用 <code>vm.$mount()</code> 手动地挂载一个未挂载的实例。</p>
<p>如果没有提供 <code>elementOrSelector</code> 参数，模板将被渲染为文档之外的的元素，并且你必须使用原生 DOM API 把它插入文档中。</p>
<p>这个方法返回实例自身，因而可以链式调用其它实例方法。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-v">MyComponent</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">extend</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">template</span>: <span class="pl-s">'&lt;div&gt;Hello!&lt;/div&gt;'</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 创建并挂载到 #app (会替换 #app)</span>
<span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">MyComponent</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$mount</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'#app'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 同上</span>
<span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">MyComponent</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">el</span>: <span class="pl-s">'#app'</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 或者，在文档之外渲染并且随后挂载</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">component</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">MyComponent</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$mount</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-smi">document</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">getElementById</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'app'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">appendChild</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">component</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">$el</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/instance.html#%E7%94%9F%E5%91%BD%E5%91%A8%E6%9C%9F%E5%9B%BE%E7%A4%BA">生命周期图示</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/ssr.html">服务端渲染</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
