<h3><a id="user-content-vmforceupdate" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmforceupdate"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$forceUpdate()</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<p>迫使 Vue 实例重新渲染。注意它仅仅影响实例本身和插入插槽内容的子组件，而不是所有子组件。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmnexttick-callback-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmnexttick-callback-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$nextTick( [callback] )</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>{Function} [callback]</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>将回调延迟到下次 DOM 更新循环之后执行。在修改数据之后立即使用它，然后等待 DOM 更新。它跟全局方法 <code>Vue.nextTick</code> 一样，不同的是回调的 <code>this</code> 自动绑定到调用它的实例上。</p>
<blockquote>
<p>2.1.0 起新增：如果没有提供回调且在支持 Promise 的环境中，则返回一个 Promise。请注意 Vue 不自带 Promise 的 polyfill，所以如果你的目标浏览器不是原生支持 Promise (IE：你们都看我干嘛)，你得自行 polyfill。</p>
</blockquote>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">methods</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
    <span class="pl-en">example</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c">// 修改数据</span>
      <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">message</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'changed'</span>
      <span class="pl-c">// DOM 还没有更新</span>
      <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$nextTick</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c">// DOM 现在更新了</span>
        <span class="pl-c">// `this` 绑定到当前实例</span>
        <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">doSomethingElse</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#Vue-nextTick">Vue.nextTick</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/reactivity.html#%E5%BC%82%E6%AD%A5%E6%9B%B4%E6%96%B0%E9%98%9F%E5%88%97">异步更新队列</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-vmdestroy" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vmdestroy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>vm.$destroy()</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>完全销毁一个实例。清理它与其它实例的连接，解绑它的全部指令及事件监听器。</p>
<p>触发 <code>beforeDestroy</code> 和 <code>destroyed</code> 的钩子。</p>
<p>在大多数场景中你不应该调用这个方法。最好使用 `v-if` 和 `v-for` 指令以数据驱动的方式控制子组件的生命周期。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/instance.html#%E7%94%9F%E5%91%BD%E5%91%A8%E6%9C%9F%E5%9B%BE%E7%A4%BA">生命周期图示</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-指令" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#指令"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>指令</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-v-text" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#v-text"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>v-text</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>预期</strong>：<code>string</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>更新元素的 <code>textContent</code>。如果要更新部分的 <code>textContent</code>，需要使用 <code>{% raw %}{{ Mustache }}{% endraw %}</code> 插值。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">span</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-text</span>="<span class="pl-s">msg</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">span</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 和下面的一样 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">span</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>{{msg}}<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">span</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/syntax.html#%E6%8F%92%E5%80%BC">数据绑定语法 - 插值</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-v-html" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#v-html"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>v-html</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>预期</strong>：<code>string</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>更新元素的 <code>innerHTML</code>。<strong>注意：内容按普通 HTML 插入 - 不会作为 Vue 模板进行编译</strong>。如果试图使用 <code>v-html</code> 组合模板，可以重新考虑是否通过使用组件来替代。</p>
<p>在网站上动态渲染任意 HTML 是非常危险的，因为容易导致 [XSS 攻击](<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cross-site_scripting)。只在可信内容上使用" rel="nofollow">https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cross-site_scripting)。只在可信内容上使用</a> `v-html`，**永不**用在用户提交的内容上。</p>
<p>在[单文件组件](../guide/single-file-components.html)里，`scoped` 的样式不会应用在 `v-html` 内部，因为那部分 HTML 没有被 Vue 的模板编译器处理。如果你希望针对 `v-html` 的内容设置带作用域的 CSS，你可以替换为 [CSS Modules](<a href="https://vue-loader.vuejs.org/en/features/css-modules.html" rel="nofollow">https://vue-loader.vuejs.org/en/features/css-modules.html</a>) 或用一个额外的全局 `&lt;style&gt;` 元素手动设置类似 BEM 的作用域策略。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-html</span>="<span class="pl-s">html</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/syntax.html#%E7%BA%AF-HTML">数据绑定语法 - 插值</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-v-show" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#v-show"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>v-show</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>预期</strong>：<code>any</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>根据表达式之真假值，切换元素的 <code>display</code> CSS property。</p>
<p>当条件变化时该指令触发过渡效果。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/conditional.html#v-show">条件渲染 - v-show</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-v-if" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#v-if"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>v-if</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>预期</strong>：<code>any</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>根据表达式的值的 <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/zh-CN/docs/Glossary/Truthy" rel="nofollow">truthiness</a> 来有条件地渲染元素。在切换时元素及它的数据绑定 / 组件被销毁并重建。如果元素是 <code>&lt;template&gt;</code>，将提出它的内容作为条件块。</p>
<p>当条件变化时该指令触发过渡效果。</p>
<p>当和 `v-if` 一起使用时，`v-for` 的优先级比 `v-if` 更高。详见[列表渲染教程](../guide/list.html#v-for-with-v-if)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/conditional.html">条件渲染 - v-if</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-v-else" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#v-else"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>v-else</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>不需要表达式</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>限制</strong>：前一兄弟元素必须有 <code>v-if</code> 或 <code>v-else-if</code>。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>为 <code>v-if</code> 或者 <code>v-else-if</code> 添加“else 块”。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-if</span>="<span class="pl-s">Math.random() &gt; 0.5</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  Now you see me
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-else</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  Now you don't
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/conditional.html#v-else">条件渲染 - v-else</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-v-else-if" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#v-else-if"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>v-else-if</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>2.1.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>类型</strong>：<code>any</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>限制</strong>：前一兄弟元素必须有 <code>v-if</code> 或 <code>v-else-if</code>。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>表示 <code>v-if</code> 的“else if 块”。可以链式调用。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-if</span>="<span class="pl-s">type === 'A'</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  A
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-else-if</span>="<span class="pl-s">type === 'B'</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  B
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-else-if</span>="<span class="pl-s">type === 'C'</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  C
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-else</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  Not A/B/C
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/conditional.html#v-else-if">条件渲染 - v-else-if</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-v-for" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#v-for"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>v-for</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>预期</strong>：<code>Array | Object | number | string | Iterable (2.6 新增)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>基于源数据多次渲染元素或模板块。此指令之值，必须使用特定语法 <code>alias in expression</code>，为当前遍历的元素提供别名：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-for</span>="<span class="pl-s">item in items</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  {{ item.text }}
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p>另外也可以为数组索引指定别名 (或者用于对象的键)：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-for</span>="<span class="pl-s">(item, index) in items</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-for</span>="<span class="pl-s">(val, key) in object</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-for</span>="<span class="pl-s">(val, name, index) in object</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p><code>v-for</code> 的默认行为会尝试原地修改元素而不是移动它们。要强制其重新排序元素，你需要用特殊 attribute <code>key</code> 来提供一个排序提示：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-for</span>="<span class="pl-s">item in items</span>" <span class="pl-c1">:key</span>="<span class="pl-s">item.id</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  {{ item.text }}
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p>从 2.6 起，<code>v-for</code> 也可以在实现了<a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/zh-CN/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Iteration_protocols#%E5%8F%AF%E8%BF%AD%E4%BB%A3%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE" rel="nofollow">可迭代协议</a>的值上使用，包括原生的 <code>Map</code> 和 <code>Set</code>。不过应该注意的是 Vue 2.x 目前并不支持可响应的 <code>Map</code> 和 <code>Set</code> 值，所以无法自动探测变更。</p>
<p>当和 `v-if` 一起使用时，`v-for` 的优先级比 `v-if` 更高。详见[列表渲染教程](../guide/list.html#v-for-with-v-if)</p>
<p><code>v-for</code> 的详细用法可以通过以下链接查看教程详细说明。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/list.html">列表渲染</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/list.html#key">key</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-v-on" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#v-on"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>v-on</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>缩写</strong>：<code>@</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>预期</strong>：<code>Function | Inline Statement | Object</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：<code>event</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>修饰符</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>.stop</code> - 调用 <code>event.stopPropagation()</code>。</li>
<li><code>.prevent</code> - 调用 <code>event.preventDefault()</code>。</li>
<li><code>.capture</code> - 添加事件侦听器时使用 capture 模式。</li>
<li><code>.self</code> - 只当事件是从侦听器绑定的元素本身触发时才触发回调。</li>
<li><code>.{keyCode | keyAlias}</code> - 只当事件是从特定键触发时才触发回调。</li>
<li><code>.native</code> - 监听组件根元素的原生事件。</li>
<li><code>.once</code> - 只触发一次回调。</li>
<li><code>.left</code> - (2.2.0) 只当点击鼠标左键时触发。</li>
<li><code>.right</code> - (2.2.0) 只当点击鼠标右键时触发。</li>
<li><code>.middle</code> - (2.2.0) 只当点击鼠标中键时触发。</li>
<li><code>.passive</code> - (2.3.0) 以 <code>{ passive: true }</code> 模式添加侦听器</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>绑定事件监听器。事件类型由参数指定。表达式可以是一个方法的名字或一个内联语句，如果没有修饰符也可以省略。</p>
<p>用在普通元素上时，只能监听<a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/zh-CN/docs/Web/Events" rel="nofollow"><strong>原生 DOM 事件</strong></a>。用在自定义元素组件上时，也可以监听子组件触发的<strong>自定义事件</strong>。</p>
<p>在监听原生 DOM 事件时，方法以事件为唯一的参数。如果使用内联语句，语句可以访问一个 <code>$event</code> property：<code>v-on:click="handle('ok', $event)"</code>。</p>
<p>从 <code>2.4.0</code> 开始，<code>v-on</code> 同样支持不带参数绑定一个事件/监听器键值对的对象。注意当使用对象语法时，是不支持任何修饰器的。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 方法处理器 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-on:click</span>="<span class="pl-s">doThis</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 动态事件 (2.6.0+) --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-on:[event]</span>="<span class="pl-s">doThis</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 内联语句 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-on:click</span>="<span class="pl-s">doThat('hello', $event)</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 缩写 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">@click</span>="<span class="pl-s">doThis</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 动态事件缩写 (2.6.0+) --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">@[event]</span>="<span class="pl-s">doThis</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 停止冒泡 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">@click.stop</span>="<span class="pl-s">doThis</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 阻止默认行为 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">@click.prevent</span>="<span class="pl-s">doThis</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 阻止默认行为，没有表达式 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">form</span> <span class="pl-c1">@submit.prevent</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">form</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!--  串联修饰符 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">@click.stop.prevent</span>="<span class="pl-s">doThis</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 键修饰符，键别名 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">input</span> <span class="pl-c1">@keyup.enter</span>="<span class="pl-s">onEnter</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 键修饰符，键代码 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">input</span> <span class="pl-c1">@keyup.13</span>="<span class="pl-s">onEnter</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 点击回调只会触发一次 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-on:click.once</span>="<span class="pl-s">doThis</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 对象语法 (2.4.0+) --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-on</span>="<span class="pl-s">{ mousedown: doThis, mouseup: doThat }</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p>在子组件上监听自定义事件 (当子组件触发“my-event”时将调用事件处理器)：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">my-component</span> <span class="pl-c1">@my-event</span>="<span class="pl-s">handleThis</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">my-component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 内联语句 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">my-component</span> <span class="pl-c1">@my-event</span>="<span class="pl-s">handleThis(123, $event)</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">my-component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 组件中的原生事件 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">my-component</span> <span class="pl-c1">@click.native</span>="<span class="pl-s">onClick</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">my-component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/events.html">事件处理器</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components.html#%E7%9B%91%E5%90%AC%E5%AD%90%E7%BB%84%E4%BB%B6%E4%BA%8B%E4%BB%B6">组件 - 自定义事件</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-v-bind" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#v-bind"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>v-bind</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>缩写</strong>：<code>:</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>预期</strong>：<code>any (with argument) | Object (without argument)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：<code>attrOrProp (optional)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>修饰符</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>.prop</code> - 作为一个 DOM property 绑定而不是作为 attribute 绑定。(<a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/6003819/properties-and-attributes-in-html#answer-6004028" rel="nofollow">差别在哪里？</a>)</li>
<li><code>.camel</code> - (2.1.0+) 将 kebab-case attribute 名转换为 camelCase。(从 2.1.0 开始支持)</li>
<li><code>.sync</code> (2.3.0+) 语法糖，会扩展成一个更新父组件绑定值的 <code>v-on</code> 侦听器。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>动态地绑定一个或多个 attribute，或一个组件 prop 到表达式。</p>
<p>在绑定 <code>class</code> 或 <code>style</code> attribute 时，支持其它类型的值，如数组或对象。可以通过下面的教程链接查看详情。</p>
<p>在绑定 prop 时，prop 必须在子组件中声明。可以用修饰符指定不同的绑定类型。</p>
<p>没有参数时，可以绑定到一个包含键值对的对象。注意此时 <code>class</code> 和 <code>style</code> 绑定不支持数组和对象。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 绑定一个 attribute --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">img</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-bind:src</span>="<span class="pl-s">imageSrc</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 动态 attribute 名 (2.6.0+) --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-bind:[key]</span>="<span class="pl-s">value</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 缩写 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">img</span> <span class="pl-c1">:src</span>="<span class="pl-s">imageSrc</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 动态 attribute 名缩写 (2.6.0+) --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">:[key]</span>="<span class="pl-s">value</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 内联字符串拼接 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">img</span> <span class="pl-c1">:src</span>="<span class="pl-s">'/path/to/images/' + fileName</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- class 绑定 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">:class</span>="<span class="pl-s">{ red: isRed }</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">:class</span>="<span class="pl-s">[classA, classB]</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">:class</span>="<span class="pl-s">[classA, { classB: isB, classC: isC }]</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- style 绑定 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">:style</span>="<span class="pl-s">{ fontSize: size + 'px' }</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">:style</span>="<span class="pl-s">[styleObjectA, styleObjectB]</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 绑定一个全是 attribute 的对象 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-bind</span>="<span class="pl-s">{ id: someProp, 'other-attr': otherProp }</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 通过 prop 修饰符绑定 DOM attribute --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-bind:text-content.prop</span>="<span class="pl-s">text</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- prop 绑定。“prop”必须在 my-component 中声明。--&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">my-component</span> <span class="pl-c1">:prop</span>="<span class="pl-s">someThing</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">my-component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 通过 $props 将父组件的 props 一起传给子组件 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">child-component</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-bind</span>="<span class="pl-s">$props</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">child-component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- XLink --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">svg</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">:xlink:special</span>="<span class="pl-s">foo</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">a</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">svg</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p><code>.camel</code> 修饰符允许在使用 DOM 模板时将 <code>v-bind</code> property 名称驼峰化，例如 SVG 的 <code>viewBox</code> property：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">svg</span> <span class="pl-c1">:view-box.camel</span>="<span class="pl-s">viewBox</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">svg</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p>在使用字符串模板或通过 <code>vue-loader</code>/<code>vueify</code> 编译时，无需使用 <code>.camel</code>。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/class-and-style.html">Class 与 Style 绑定</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components.html#%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87-Prop-%E5%90%91%E5%AD%90%E7%BB%84%E4%BB%B6%E4%BC%A0%E9%80%92%E6%95%B0%E6%8D%AE">组件 - Props</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-custom-events.html#sync-%E4%BF%AE%E9%A5%B0%E7%AC%A6">组件 - <code>.sync</code> 修饰符</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-v-model" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#v-model"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>v-model</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>预期</strong>：随表单控件类型不同而不同。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>限制</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>&lt;input&gt;</code></li>
<li><code>&lt;select&gt;</code></li>
<li><code>&lt;textarea&gt;</code></li>
<li>components</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>修饰符</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/forms.html#lazy"><code>.lazy</code></a> - 取代 <code>input</code> 监听 <code>change</code> 事件</li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/forms.html#number"><code>.number</code></a> - 输入字符串转为有效的数字</li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/forms.html#trim"><code>.trim</code></a> - 输入首尾空格过滤</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>在表单控件或者组件上创建双向绑定。细节请看下面的教程链接。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/forms.html">表单控件绑定</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-custom-events.html#%E5%B0%86%E5%8E%9F%E7%94%9F%E4%BA%8B%E4%BB%B6%E7%BB%91%E5%AE%9A%E5%88%B0%E7%BB%84%E4%BB%B6">组件 - 在输入组件上使用自定义事件</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-v-slot" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#v-slot"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>v-slot</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>缩写</strong>：<code>#</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>预期</strong>：可放置在函数参数位置的 JavaScript 表达式 (在<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-slots.html#%E8%A7%A3%E6%9E%84%E6%8F%92%E6%A7%BD-Props">支持的环境下</a>可使用解构)。可选，即只需要在为插槽传入 prop 的时候使用。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参数</strong>：插槽名 (可选，默认值是 <code>default</code>)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>限用于</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><code>&lt;template&gt;</code></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-slots.html#%E7%8B%AC%E5%8D%A0%E9%BB%98%E8%AE%A4%E6%8F%92%E6%A7%BD%E7%9A%84%E7%BC%A9%E5%86%99%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95">组件</a> (对于一个单独的带 prop 的默认插槽)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>提供具名插槽或需要接收 prop 的插槽。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 具名插槽 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">base-layout</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">template</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-slot:header</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
    Header content
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">template</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

  Default slot content

  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">template</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-slot:footer</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
    Footer content
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">template</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">base-layout</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 接收 prop 的具名插槽 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">infinite-scroll</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">template</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-slot:item</span>="<span class="pl-s">slotProps</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">item</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
      {{ slotProps.item.text }}
    <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">template</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">infinite-scroll</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 接收 prop 的默认插槽，使用了解构 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">mouse-position</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-slot</span>="<span class="pl-s">{ x, y }</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  Mouse position: {{ x }}, {{ y }}
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">mouse-position</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p>更多细节请查阅以下链接。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-slots.html">组件 - 插槽</a></li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/vuejs/rfcs/blob/master/active-rfcs/0001-new-slot-syntax.md">RFC-0001</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-v-pre" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#v-pre"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>v-pre</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>不需要表达式</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>跳过这个元素和它的子元素的编译过程。可以用来显示原始 Mustache 标签。跳过大量没有指令的节点会加快编译。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">span</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-pre</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>{{ this will not be compiled }}<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">span</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-v-cloak" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#v-cloak"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>v-cloak</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>不需要表达式</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>这个指令保持在元素上直到关联实例结束编译。和 CSS 规则如 <code>[v-cloak] { display: none }</code> 一起用时，这个指令可以隐藏未编译的 Mustache 标签直到实例准备完毕。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-css"><pre>[<span class="pl-c1">v-cloak</span>] {
  <span class="pl-c1">display</span>: none;
}</pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-cloak</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  {{ message }}
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<div> 不会显示，直到编译结束。
</div></li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-v-once" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#v-once"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>v-once</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>不需要表达式</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>详细</strong>：</p>
<p>只渲染元素和组件<strong>一次</strong>。随后的重新渲染，元素/组件及其所有的子节点将被视为静态内容并跳过。这可以用于优化更新性能。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 单个元素 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">span</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-once</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>This will never change: {{msg}}<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">span</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 有子元素 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-once</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>comment<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>{{msg}}<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 组件 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">my-component</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-once</span> <span class="pl-c1">:comment</span>="<span class="pl-s">msg</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">my-component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- `v-for` 指令--&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">ul</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">li</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-for</span>="<span class="pl-s">i in list</span>" <span class="pl-c1">v-once</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>{{i}}<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">li</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">ul</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/syntax.html#%E6%8F%92%E5%80%BC">数据绑定语法- 插值</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-edge-cases.html#%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87-v-once-%E5%88%9B%E5%BB%BA%E4%BD%8E%E5%BC%80%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E9%9D%99%E6%80%81%E7%BB%84%E4%BB%B6">组件 - 对低开销的静态组件使用 <code>v-once</code></a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-特殊-attribute" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#特殊-attribute"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>特殊 attribute</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-key" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#key"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>key</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>预期</strong>：<code>number | string | boolean (2.4.2 新增) | symbol (2.5.12 新增)</code></p>
<p><code>key</code> 的特殊 attribute 主要用在 Vue 的虚拟 DOM 算法，在新旧 nodes 对比时辨识 VNodes。如果不使用 key，Vue 会使用一种最大限度减少动态元素并且尽可能的尝试就地修改/复用相同类型元素的算法。而使用 key 时，它会基于 key 的变化重新排列元素顺序，并且会移除 key 不存在的元素。</p>
<p>有相同父元素的子元素必须有<strong>独特的 key</strong>。重复的 key 会造成渲染错误。</p>
<p>最常见的用例是结合 <code>v-for</code>：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">ul</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">li</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-for</span>="<span class="pl-s">item in items</span>" <span class="pl-c1">:key</span>="<span class="pl-s">item.id</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>...<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">li</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">ul</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p>它也可以用于强制替换元素/组件而不是重复使用它。当你遇到如下场景时它可能会很有用：</p>
<ul>
<li>完整地触发组件的生命周期钩子</li>
<li>触发过渡</li>
</ul>
<p>例如：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">transition</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">span</span> <span class="pl-c1">:key</span>="<span class="pl-s">text</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>{{ text }}<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">span</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">transition</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p>当 <code>text</code> 发生改变时，<code>&lt;span&gt;</code> 总是会被替换而不是被修改，因此会触发过渡。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-ref" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#ref"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>ref</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>预期</strong>：<code>string</code></p>
<p><code>ref</code> 被用来给元素或子组件注册引用信息。引用信息将会注册在父组件的 <code>$refs</code> 对象上。如果在普通的 DOM 元素上使用，引用指向的就是 DOM 元素；如果用在子组件上，引用就指向组件实例：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- `vm.$refs.p` will be the DOM node --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span> <span class="pl-c1">ref</span>="<span class="pl-s">p</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>hello<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- `vm.$refs.child` will be the child component instance --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">child-component</span> <span class="pl-c1">ref</span>="<span class="pl-s">child</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">child-component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p>当 <code>v-for</code> 用于元素或组件的时候，引用信息将是包含 DOM 节点或组件实例的数组。</p>
<p>关于 ref 注册时间的重要说明：因为 ref 本身是作为渲染结果被创建的，在初始渲染的时候你不能访问它们 - 它们还不存在！<code>$refs</code> 也不是响应式的，因此你不应该试图用它在模板中做数据绑定。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-edge-cases.html#%E8%AE%BF%E9%97%AE%E5%AD%90%E7%BB%84%E4%BB%B6%E5%AE%9E%E4%BE%8B%E6%88%96%E5%AD%90%E5%85%83%E7%B4%A0">子组件 ref</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-is" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#is"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>is</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>预期</strong>：<code>string | Object (组件的选项对象)</code></li>
</ul>
<p> 用于<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components.html#%E5%8A%A8%E6%80%81%E7%BB%84%E4%BB%B6">动态组件</a>且基于 <a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components.html#%E8%A7%A3%E6%9E%90-DOM-%E6%A8%A1%E6%9D%BF%E6%97%B6%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%A8%E6%84%8F%E4%BA%8B%E9%A1%B9">DOM 内模板的限制</a>来工作。</p>
<p>示例：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 当 `currentView` 改变时，组件也跟着改变 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-bind:is</span>="<span class="pl-s">currentView</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 这样做是有必要的，因为 `&lt;my-row&gt;` 放在一个 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- `&lt;table&gt;` 内可能无效且被放置到外面 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">table</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">tr</span> <span class="pl-c1">is</span>="<span class="pl-s">my-row</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">tr</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">table</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p>更多的使用细节，请移步至下面的链接。</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>See also</strong>：
<ul>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components.html#%E5%8A%A8%E6%80%81%E7%BB%84%E4%BB%B6">动态组件</a></li>
<li><a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components.html#%E8%A7%A3%E6%9E%90-DOM-%E6%A8%A1%E6%9D%BF%E6%97%B6%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%A8%E6%84%8F%E4%BA%8B%E9%A1%B9">DOM 模板解析说明</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-slot-废弃" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#slot-废弃"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>slot <sup>废弃</sup></h3>
<p><strong>推荐 2.6.0 新增的 <a href="#v-slot">v-slot</a>。</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>预期</strong>：<code>string</code></p>
<p>用于标记往哪个具名插槽中插入子组件内容。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-slots.html#%E5%85%B7%E5%90%8D%E6%8F%92%E6%A7%BD">具名插槽</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-slot-scope-废弃" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#slot-scope-废弃"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>slot-scope <sup>废弃</sup></h3>
<p><strong>推荐 2.6.0 新增的 <a href="#v-slot">v-slot</a>。</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>预期</strong>：<code>function argument expression</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>用于将元素或组件表示为作用域插槽。attribute 的值应该是可以出现在函数签名的参数位置的合法的 JavaScript 表达式。这意味着在支持的环境中，你还可以在表达式中使用 ES2015 解构。它在 2.5.0+ 中替代了 <a href="#scope-replaced"><code>scope</code></a>。</p>
<p>此 attribute 不支持动态绑定。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-slots.html#%E4%BD%9C%E7%94%A8%E5%9F%9F%E6%8F%92%E6%A7%BD">作用域插槽</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-scope-移除" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#scope-移除"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>scope <sup>移除</sup></h3>
<p><strong>被 2.5.0 新增的 <a href="#slot-scope">slot-scope</a> 取代。推荐 2.6.0 新增的 <a href="#v-slot">v-slot</a>。</strong></p>
<p>用于表示一个作为带作用域的插槽的 <code>&lt;template&gt;</code> 元素，它在 2.5.0+ 中被 <a href="#slot-scope"><code>slot-scope</code></a> 替代。</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>用法：</strong></p>
<p>除了 <code>scope</code> 只可以用于 <code>&lt;template&gt;</code> 元素，其它和 <a href="#slot-scope"><code>slot-scope</code></a> 都相同。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-内置的组件" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#内置的组件"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>内置的组件</h2>
<h3><a id="user-content-component" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#component"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>component</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Props</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>is</code> - string | ComponentDefinition | ComponentConstructor</li>
<li><code>inline-template</code> - boolean</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p>渲染一个“元组件”为动态组件。依 <code>is</code> 的值，来决定哪个组件被渲染。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 动态组件由 vm 实例的 `componentId` property 控制 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span> <span class="pl-c1">:is</span>="<span class="pl-s">componentId</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 也能够渲染注册过的组件或 prop 传入的组件 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span> <span class="pl-c1">:is</span>="<span class="pl-s">$options.components.child</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components.html#%E5%8A%A8%E6%80%81%E7%BB%84%E4%BB%B6">动态组件</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-transition" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#transition"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>transition</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Props</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>name</code> - string，用于自动生成 CSS 过渡类名。例如：<code>name: 'fade'</code> 将自动拓展为 <code>.fade-enter</code>，<code>.fade-enter-active</code> 等。默认类名为 <code>"v"</code></li>
<li><code>appear</code> - boolean，是否在初始渲染时使用过渡。默认为 <code>false</code>。</li>
<li><code>css</code> - boolean，是否使用 CSS 过渡类。默认为 <code>true</code>。如果设置为 <code>false</code>，将只通过组件事件触发注册的 JavaScript 钩子。</li>
<li><code>type</code> - string，指定过渡事件类型，侦听过渡何时结束。有效值为 <code>"transition"</code> 和 <code>"animation"</code>。默认 Vue.js 将自动检测出持续时间长的为过渡事件类型。</li>
<li><code>mode</code> - string，控制离开/进入过渡的时间序列。有效的模式有 <code>"out-in"</code> 和 <code>"in-out"</code>；默认同时进行。</li>
<li><code>duration</code> - number | { <code>enter</code>: number, <code>leave</code>: number } 指定过渡的持续时间。默认情况下，Vue 会等待过渡所在根元素的第一个 <code>transitionend</code> 或 <code>animationend</code> 事件。</li>
<li><code>enter-class</code> - string</li>
<li><code>leave-class</code> - string</li>
<li><code>appear-class</code> - string</li>
<li><code>enter-to-class</code> - string</li>
<li><code>leave-to-class</code> - string</li>
<li><code>appear-to-class</code> - string</li>
<li><code>enter-active-class</code> - string</li>
<li><code>leave-active-class</code> - string</li>
<li><code>appear-active-class</code> - string</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>事件</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>before-enter</code></li>
<li><code>before-leave</code></li>
<li><code>before-appear</code></li>
<li><code>enter</code></li>
<li><code>leave</code></li>
<li><code>appear</code></li>
<li><code>after-enter</code></li>
<li><code>after-leave</code></li>
<li><code>after-appear</code></li>
<li><code>enter-cancelled</code></li>
<li><code>leave-cancelled</code> (<code>v-show</code> only)</li>
<li><code>appear-cancelled</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p><code>&lt;transition&gt;</code> 元素作为<strong>单个</strong>元素/组件的过渡效果。<code>&lt;transition&gt;</code> 只会把过渡效果应用到其包裹的内容上，而不会额外渲染 DOM 元素，也不会出现在可被检查的组件层级中。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 简单元素 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">transition</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-if</span>="<span class="pl-s">ok</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>toggled content<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">transition</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 动态组件 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">transition</span> <span class="pl-c1">name</span>="<span class="pl-s">fade</span>" <span class="pl-c1">mode</span>="<span class="pl-s">out-in</span>" <span class="pl-c1">appear</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span> <span class="pl-c1">:is</span>="<span class="pl-s">view</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">transition</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 事件钩子 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span>="<span class="pl-s">transition-demo</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">transition</span> <span class="pl-c1">@after-enter</span>="<span class="pl-s">transitionComplete</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-show</span>="<span class="pl-s">ok</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>toggled content<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">transition</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js"><pre><span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Vue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  ...
  <span class="pl-s1">methods</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-en">transitionComplete</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">el</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c">// 传入 'el' 这个 DOM 元素作为参数。</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">$mount</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'#transition-demo'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/transitions.html">过渡：进入，离开和列表</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-transition-group" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#transition-group"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>transition-group</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Props</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>tag</code> - string，默认为 <code>span</code></li>
<li><code>move-class</code> - 覆盖移动过渡期间应用的 CSS 类。</li>
<li>除了 <code>mode</code>，其他 attribute 和 <code>&lt;transition&gt;</code> 相同。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>事件</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li>事件和 <code>&lt;transition&gt;</code> 相同。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p><code>&lt;transition-group&gt;</code> 元素作为多个元素/组件的过渡效果。<code>&lt;transition-group&gt;</code> 渲染一个真实的 DOM 元素。默认渲染 <code>&lt;span&gt;</code>，可以通过 <code>tag</code> attribute 配置哪个元素应该被渲染。</p>
<p>注意，每个 <code>&lt;transition-group&gt;</code> 的子节点必须有<strong>独立的 key</strong>，动画才能正常工作</p>
<p><code>&lt;transition-group&gt;</code> 支持通过 CSS transform 过渡移动。当一个子节点被更新，从屏幕上的位置发生变化，它会被应用一个移动中的 CSS 类 (通过 <code>name</code> attribute 或配置 <code>move-class</code> attribute 自动生成)。如果 CSS <code>transform</code> property 是“可过渡”property，当应用移动类时，将会使用 <a href="https://aerotwist.com/blog/flip-your-animations/" rel="nofollow">FLIP 技术</a>使元素流畅地到达动画终点。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">transition-group</span> <span class="pl-c1">tag</span>="<span class="pl-s">ul</span>" <span class="pl-c1">name</span>="<span class="pl-s">slide</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">li</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-for</span>="<span class="pl-s">item in items</span>" <span class="pl-c1">:key</span>="<span class="pl-s">item.id</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
    {{ item.text }}
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">li</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">transition-group</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/transitions.html">过渡：进入，离开和列表</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-keep-alive" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#keep-alive"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>keep-alive</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Props</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>include</code> - 字符串或正则表达式。只有名称匹配的组件会被缓存。</li>
<li><code>exclude</code> - 字符串或正则表达式。任何名称匹配的组件都不会被缓存。</li>
<li><code>max</code> - 数字。最多可以缓存多少组件实例。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>用法</strong>：</p>
<p><code>&lt;keep-alive&gt;</code> 包裹动态组件时，会缓存不活动的组件实例，而不是销毁它们。和 <code>&lt;transition&gt;</code> 相似，<code>&lt;keep-alive&gt;</code> 是一个抽象组件：它自身不会渲染一个 DOM 元素，也不会出现在组件的父组件链中。</p>
<p>当组件在 <code>&lt;keep-alive&gt;</code> 内被切换，它的 <code>activated</code> 和 <code>deactivated</code> 这两个生命周期钩子函数将会被对应执行。</p>
<blockquote>
<p>在 2.2.0 及其更高版本中，<code>activated</code> 和 <code>deactivated</code> 将会在 <code>&lt;keep-alive&gt;</code> 树内的所有嵌套组件中触发。</p>
</blockquote>
<p>主要用于保留组件状态或避免重新渲染。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 基本 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">keep-alive</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span> <span class="pl-c1">:is</span>="<span class="pl-s">view</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">keep-alive</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 多个条件判断的子组件 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">keep-alive</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">comp-a</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-if</span>="<span class="pl-s">a &gt; 1</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">comp-a</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">comp-b</span> <span class="pl-c1">v-else</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">comp-b</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">keep-alive</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 和 `&lt;transition&gt;` 一起使用 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">transition</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">keep-alive</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span> <span class="pl-c1">:is</span>="<span class="pl-s">view</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">keep-alive</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">transition</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p>注意，<code>&lt;keep-alive&gt;</code> 是用在其一个直属的子组件被开关的情形。如果你在其中有 <code>v-for</code> 则不会工作。如果有上述的多个条件性的子元素，<code>&lt;keep-alive&gt;</code> 要求同时只有一个子元素被渲染。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong><code>include</code> and <code>exclude</code></strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p>2.1.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<p><code>include</code> 和 <code>exclude</code> prop 允许组件有条件地缓存。二者都可以用逗号分隔字符串、正则表达式或一个数组来表示：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 逗号分隔字符串 --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">keep-alive</span> <span class="pl-c1">include</span>="<span class="pl-s">a,b</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span> <span class="pl-c1">:is</span>="<span class="pl-s">view</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">keep-alive</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 正则表达式 (使用 `v-bind`) --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">keep-alive</span> <span class="pl-c1">:include</span>="<span class="pl-s">/a|b/</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span> <span class="pl-c1">:is</span>="<span class="pl-s">view</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">keep-alive</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- 数组 (使用 `v-bind`) --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">keep-alive</span> <span class="pl-c1">:include</span>="<span class="pl-s">['a', 'b']</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span> <span class="pl-c1">:is</span>="<span class="pl-s">view</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">keep-alive</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p>匹配首先检查组件自身的 <code>name</code> 选项，如果 <code>name</code> 选项不可用，则匹配它的局部注册名称 (父组件 <code>components</code> 选项的键值)。匿名组件不能被匹配。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong><code>max</code></strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p>2.5.0 新增</p>
</blockquote>
<p>最多可以缓存多少组件实例。一旦这个数字达到了，在新实例被创建之前，已缓存组件中最久没有被访问的实例会被销毁掉。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">keep-alive</span> <span class="pl-c1">:max</span>="<span class="pl-s">10</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span> <span class="pl-c1">:is</span>="<span class="pl-s">view</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">component</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">keep-alive</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p>`` 不会在函数式组件中正常工作，因为它们没有缓存实例。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components-dynamic-async.html#%E5%9C%A8%E5%8A%A8%E6%80%81%E7%BB%84%E4%BB%B6%E4%B8%8A%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8-keep-alive">动态组件 - keep-alive</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-slot" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#slot"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>slot</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Props</strong>：</p>
<ul>
<li><code>name</code> - string，用于命名插槽。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Usage</strong>：</p>
<p><code>&lt;slot&gt;</code> 元素作为组件模板之中的内容分发插槽。<code>&lt;slot&gt;</code> 元素自身将被替换。</p>
<p>详细用法，请参考下面教程的链接。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>参考</strong>：<a href="/vuejs/cn.vuejs.org/blob/master/src/v2/guide/components.html#%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87%E6%8F%92%E6%A7%BD%E5%88%86%E5%8F%91%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9">通过插槽分发内容</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-vnode-接口" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#vnode-接口"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>VNode 接口</h2>
<ul>
<li>请参考 <a href="https://github.com/vuejs/vue/blob/dev/src/core/vdom/vnode.js">VNode class declaration</a>。</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-服务端渲染" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#服务端渲染"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>服务端渲染</h2>
